<h5> <span class="mw-headline" id=".2AFor_Medium_Voice.2C_Clarinet_and_Strings_.28Mondrup.29">*For Medium Voice, Clarinet and Strings (Mondrup)</span></h5>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Biblical Songs
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">Biblické písně
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Dvo%C5%99%C3%A1k,_Anton%C3%ADn" title="Category:Dvořák, Antonín">Dvořák, Antonín</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>Op.99&#160;; B.185
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IAD 8
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>10 songs
<ol><li> Oblak a mrákota jest vůkol Něho. Andantino (B major)
</li><li> Skrýše má a paveza má Ty jsí. Andante (A minor)
</li><li> Slyš, ó Bože, slyš modlitbu mou. Andante (E-flat major)
</li><li> Hospodin jest můj pastýř. Andante (E major)
</li><li> Bože! Bože! Píseň novou. Risoluto maestoso (C major)
</li><li> Slyš, ó Bože, volání mé. Andante (G major)
</li><li> Při řekách babylonských. Andante (E minor)
</li><li> Popatřiž na mne a smiluj se nade mnou.  Andante (C minor)
</li><li> Pozdvihuji očí svých k horám. Andante con moto (A major)
</li><li> Zpívejte Hospodinu píseň novou. Allegro moderato (B-flat major)
</li></ol>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Year/Date of Composition</span><span class="ms555">Y/D of Comp.</span>
</th>
<td>1894 (March 5-26)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Perf<span class="mh555">ormance</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1895-09-26 in Mlada Boleslav
<dl><dd>O. Schellerova (voice), Unknown (piano) - <i>No.6 only</i>
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Pub<span class="mh555">lication</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1895
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Librettist
</th>
<td>The Bible of Králice (16th century)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Language
</th>
<td>Czech
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Average Duration</span><span class="ms555">Avg. Duration</span>
</th>
<td>25 minutes
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Composer Time Period</span><span class="ms555">Comp. Period</span>

<td>voice, piano
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>External Links
</th>
<td><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Biblical_Songs" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Biblical Songs">Wikipedia article</a><br /><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.antonin-dvorak.cz/en/biblical-songs">antonin-dvorak.cz</a></span><br /><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.classicalarchives.com/work/9296.html#tvf=tracks&amp;tv=about">Classical Archives article</a></span><br /><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.allmusic.com/composition/biblical-songs-biblické-p%C3%ADsne-10-for-voice-amp-piano-or-orchestra-b-185-op-99-mc0002369540">All Music Guide</a></span><br /><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.lieder.net/lieder/assemble_texts.html?SongCycleId=242">The Lied, Art Song, and Choral Texts Archive</a></span>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Extra Information
</th>
<td>Version History:
<ul><li> Composed for voice and piano, 1894
</li><li> Nos.1-5 were orchestrated by the composer, 1895. 
</li></ul>
<dl><dd>Instrumentation: soprano, 2 flutes, 2 clarinets, 2 horns, 2 trumpets, timpani, triangle, harp, strings. First published in this version in 1929, with Nos.6-10 in orchestrations by Vilém Zemánek (1875–1922).
</dd></dl>
</td></tr></table>
